[4mVISUDO[24m(8)                   System Manager's Manual                  [4mVISUDO[24m(8)[m
[m
[1mNAME[0m[m
       visudo — edit the sudoers file[m
[m
[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m
       [1mvisudo [22m[[1m-chIOPqsV[22m] [[[1m-f[22m] [4msudoers[24m][m
[m
[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       [1mvisudo  [22medits the [4msudoers[24m file in a safe fashion, analogous to [4mvipw[24m(8).[m
       [1mvisudo [22mlocks the [4msudoers[24m file against multiple simultaneous edits, per‐[m
       forms basic validity checks, and checks for syntax  errors  before  in‐[m
       stalling  the  edited  file.   If  the  [4msudoers[24m file is currently being[m
       edited you will receive a message to try again later.[m
[m
       If the [4msudoers[24m file does not exist, it will be created unless the  edi‐[m
       tor exits without writing to the file.[m
[m
       [1mvisudo  [22mparses  the  [4msudoers[24m  file  after editing and will not save the[m
       changes if there is a syntax error.  Upon finding an error, [1mvisudo [22mwill[m
       print a message stating the line number(s) where the error occurred and[m
       the user will receive the “What now?” prompt.  At this point  the  user[m
       may  enter  ‘e’ to re-edit the [4msudoers[24m file, ‘x’ to exit without saving[m
[7m Manual page visudo(8) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       the changes, or ‘Q’ to quit and save changes.  The ‘Q’ option should be[m
[7m Manual page visudo(8) line 2 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       used with extreme caution because if [1mvisudo [22mbelieves there to be a syn‐[m
[7m Manual page visudo(8) line 3 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       tax error, so will [1msudo[22m.  If ‘e’ is typed to edit the [4msudoers[24m file  af‐[m
[7m Manual page visudo(8) line 4 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       ter  a syntax error has been detected, the cursor will be placed on the[m
[7m Manual page visudo(8) line 5 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       line where the error occurred (if the editor supports this feature).[m
[7m Manual page visudo(8) line 6 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K[m
[7m Manual page visudo(8) line 7 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       There are two [4msudoers[24m settings that determine which editor [1mvisudo  [22mwill[m
[7m Manual page visudo(8) line 8 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       run.[m
[7m Manual page visudo(8) line 9 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K[m
[7m Manual page visudo(8) line 10 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       editor      A  colon (‘:’) separated list of editors allowed to be used[m
[7m Manual page visudo(8) line 11 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K                   with [1mvisudo[22m.  [1mvisudo [22mwill choose the  editor  that  matches[m
[7m Manual page visudo(8) line 12 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K                   the user's SUDO_EDITOR, VISUAL, or EDITOR environment vari‐[m
[7m Manual page visudo(8) line 13 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K

[4mCHMOD[24m(1)                         User Commands                        [4mCHMOD[24m(1)[m
[m
[1mNAME[0m[m
       chmod - change file mode bits[m
[m
[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m
       [1mchmod [22m[[4mOPTION[24m]... [4mMODE[24m[[4m,MODE[24m]... [4mFILE[24m...[m
       [1mchmod [22m[[4mOPTION[24m]... [4mOCTAL-MODE[24m [4mFILE[24m...[m
       [1mchmod [22m[[4mOPTION[24m]... [4m--reference=RFILE[24m [4mFILE[24m...[m
[m
[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       This manual page documents the GNU version of [1mchmod[22m.  [1mchmod [22mchanges the[m
       file  mode  bits of each given file according to [4mmode[24m, which can be ei‐[m
       ther a symbolic representation of changes to make, or an  octal  number[m
       representing the bit pattern for the new mode bits.[m
[m
       The  format  of a symbolic mode is [[1mugoa[22m...][[[1m-+=[22m][[4mperms[24m...]...], where[m
       [4mperms[24m is either zero or more letters from the set [1mrwxXst[22m, or  a  single[m
       letter  from  the set [1mugo[22m.  Multiple symbolic modes can be given, sepa‐[m
       rated by commas.[m
[m
       A combination of the letters [1mugoa [22mcontrols which users' access  to  the[m
       file  will  be  changed:  the  user who owns it ([1mu[22m), other users in the[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       file's group ([1mg[22m), other users not in the file's group ([1mo[22m), or all users[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 2 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       ([1ma[22m).  If none of these are given, the effect is as if ([1ma[22m)  were  given,[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 3 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       but bits that are set in the umask are not affected.[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 4 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 5 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       The  operator  [1m+  [22mcauses the selected file mode bits to be added to the[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 6 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       existing file mode bits of each file; [1m- [22mcauses them to be removed;  and[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 7 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       [1m= [22mcauses them to be added and causes unmentioned bits to be removed ex‐[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 8 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       cept  that a directory's unmentioned set user and group ID bits are not[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 9 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       affected.[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 10 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 11 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       The letters [1mrwxXst [22mselect file mode bits for the affected  users:  read[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 12 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       ([1mr[22m), write ([1mw[22m), execute (or search for directories) ([1mx[22m), execute/search[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 13 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       only  if  the file is a directory or already has execute permission for[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 14 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       some user ([1mX[22m), set user or group ID on execution ([1ms[22m), restricted  dele‐[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 15 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       tion  flag or sticky bit ([1mt[22m).  Instead of one or more of these letters,[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 16 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       you can specify exactly one of the letters [1mugo[22m: the permissions granted[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 17 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       to the user who owns the file ([1mu[22m), the  permissions  granted  to  other[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 18 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       users  who  are  members  of  the file's group ([1mg[22m), and the permissions[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 19 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       granted to users that are in neither of the  two  preceding  categories[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 20 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       ([1mo[22m).[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 21 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 22 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       A  numeric  mode  is  from  one  to four octal digits (0-7), derived by[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 23 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       adding up the bits with values 4, 2, and 1.  Omitted digits are assumed[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 24 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       to be leading zeros.  The first digit selects the set user ID  (4)  and[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 25 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       set group ID (2) and restricted deletion or sticky (1) attributes.  The[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 26 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       second  digit  selects permissions for the user who owns the file: read[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 27 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       (4), write (2), and execute (1);  the  third  selects  permissions  for[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 28 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       other  users  in the file's group, with the same values; and the fourth[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 29 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       for other users not in the file's group, with the same values.[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 30 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 31 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       [1mchmod [22mnever changes the permissions of symbolic links; the [1mchmod [22msystem[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 32 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       call cannot change their permissions.  This is not a problem since  the[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 33 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       permissions  of  symbolic links are never used.  However, for each sym‐[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 34 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       bolic link listed on the command line, [1mchmod [22mchanges the permissions of[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 35 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       the pointed-to file.  In contrast, [1mchmod [22mignores symbolic links encoun‐[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 36 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       tered during recursive directory traversals.[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 37 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 38 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K[1mSETUID AND SETGID BITS[0m[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 39 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       [1mchmod [22mclears the set-group-ID bit of a regular file if the file's group[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 40 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       ID does not match the user's effective group ID or one  of  the  user's[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 41 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       supplementary  group  IDs,  unless the user has appropriate privileges.[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 42 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       Additional restrictions may cause the set-user-ID and set-group-ID bits[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 43 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       of [4mMODE[24m or [4mRFILE[24m to be ignored.  This behavior depends  on  the  policy[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 44 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       and  functionality of the underlying [1mchmod [22msystem call.  When in doubt,[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 45 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       check the underlying system behavior.[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 46 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 47 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       For directories [1mchmod [22mpreserves set-user-ID and set-group-ID  bits  un‐[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 48 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       less  you  explicitly specify otherwise.  You can set or clear the bits[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 49 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       with symbolic modes like [1mu+s [22mand [1mg-s[22m.  To clear these bits for directo‐[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 50 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       ries with a numeric mode  requires  an  additional  leading  zero  like[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 51 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       [1m00755[22m, leading minus like [1m-6000[22m, or leading equals like [1m=755[22m.[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 52 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 53 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K[1mRESTRICTED DELETION FLAG OR STICKY BIT[0m[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 54 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       The  restricted  deletion flag or sticky bit is a single bit, whose in‐[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 55 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       terpretation depends on the file type.  For  directories,  it  prevents[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 56 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       unprivileged  users  from  removing or renaming a file in the directory[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 57 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       unless they own the file or the  directory;  this  is  called  the  [4mre‐[0m[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 58 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       [4mstricted[24m  [4mdeletion[24m  [4mflag[24m  for  the  directory, and is commonly found on[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 59 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       world-writable directories like [1m/tmp[22m.  For regular files on some  older[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 60 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       systems,  the  bit saves the program's text image on the swap device so[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 61 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       it will load more quickly when run; this is called the [4msticky[24m [4mbit[24m.[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 62 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K[m
[7m Manual page chmod(1) line 63 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB

[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       [1msudo [22mallows a permitted user to execute a [4mcommand[24m as the  superuser  or[m
       another user, as specified by the security policy.  The invoking user's[m
       real  ([4mnot[24m  effective)  user-ID is used to determine the user name with[m
       which to query the security policy.[m
[m
[7m Manual page sudo(8) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       [1msudo [22msupports a plugin architecture for  security  policies,  auditing,[m
[7m Manual page sudo(8) line 2 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB

[7m Manual page sudo(8) line 3 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K

[7m Manual page sudo(8) line 4 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB

[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB

[7m Manual page sudo(8) line 7 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB

[7m Manual page sudo(8) line 8 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       The security policy determines what privileges, if any, a user  has  to[m
[7m Manual page sudo(8) line 9 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K

[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       Security  policies  may support credential caching to allow the user to[m

[4mPS[24m(1)                            User Commands                           [4mPS[24m(1)[m

[1mNAME[0m[m
       ps - report a snapshot of the current processes.[m
[m
[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m
       [1mps [22m[[4moptions[24m][m
[m
[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       [1mps [22mdisplays information about a selection of the active processes.  If[m
       you want a repetitive update of the selection and the displayed[m
       information, use [1mtop [22minstead.[m
[m
       This version of [1mps [22maccepts several kinds of options:[m
[m
       1   UNIX options, which may be grouped and must be preceded by a dash.[m
       2   BSD options, which may be grouped and must not be used with a dash.[m
       3   GNU long options, which are preceded by two dashes.[m
[m
       Options  of  different  types  may  be  freely mixed, but conflicts can[m
       appear.  There are some  synonymous  options,  which  are  functionally[m
       identical,  due  to the many standards and [1mps [22mimplementations that this[m
       [1mps [22mis compatible with.[m
[7m Manual page ps(1) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K[m
[7m Manual page ps(1) line 2 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       By default, [1mps [22mselects all processes with the same  effective  user  ID[m
[7m Manual page ps(1) line 3 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       (euid=EUID)  as  the current user and associated with the same terminal[m
[7m Manual page ps(1) line 4 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       as the invoker.  It displays the process  ID  (pid=PID),  the  terminal[m
[7m Manual page ps(1) line 5 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       associated  with  the  process  (tname=TTY),  the cumulated CPU time in[m
[7m Manual page ps(1) line 6 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       [DD-]hh:mm:ss format (time=TIME), and the executable  name  (ucmd=CMD).[m
[7m Manual page ps(1) line 7 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       Output is unsorted by default.[m
[7m Manual page ps(1) line 8 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K[m
[7m Manual page ps(1) line 9 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       The  use of BSD-style options will add process state (stat=STAT) to the[m
[7m Manual page ps(1) line 10 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       default display and show the command args (args=COMMAND) instead of the[m
[7m Manual page ps(1) line 11 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       executable name.  You can override this with the [1mPS_FORMAT  [22menvironment[m
[7m Manual page ps(1) line 12 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       variable.   The  use  of BSD-style options will also change the process[m
[7m Manual page ps(1) line 13 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       selection to include processes on other terminals (TTYs) that are owned[m
[7m Manual page ps(1) line 14 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       by you; alternately, this may be described as setting the selection  to[m
[7m Manual page ps(1) line 15 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       be  the  set  of  all  processes filtered to exclude processes owned by[m
[7m Manual page ps(1) line 16 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       other users or not on a terminal.  These  effects  are  not  considered[m
[7m Manual page ps(1) line 17 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       when  options  are  described as being "identical" below, so [1m-M [22mwill be[m
[7m Manual page ps(1) line 18 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       considered identical to [1mZ [22mand so on.[m
[7m Manual page ps(1) line 19 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K[m
[7m Manual page ps(1) line 20 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       Except as described below, process selection options are additive.  The[m
[7m Manual page ps(1) line 21 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       default selection is discarded, and then  the  selected  processes  are[m
[7m Manual page ps(1) line 22 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       added  to the set of processes to be displayed.  A process will thus be[m
[7m Manual page ps(1) line 23 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB
[K       shown if it meets any of the given selection criteria.[m
